<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">побря́кать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pobrjákatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побрякушка.html>побряку́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobrjakúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побрякушка.html>побряку́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побрякушка.html>побряку́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побрякушка.html>побряку́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rattle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">child's toy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small pendant or ornament that jingles when it moves</li>

***побудить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:побудить.html>побуди́ть</a> (15782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будить.html>буди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">budítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побудить.html>побуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будить.html>буди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend some time awakening</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wake up (all or many people, one by one)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to awaken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hunting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drive (an animal) from its hole or lair, to flush out</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побудить.html>побуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побуждать.html>побужда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to induce, to prompt, to impel, to spur</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:побуждать.html>побужда́ть</a> (16522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побудить.html>побуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pobudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poveztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a> (5823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, to throw, to fell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring down, to topple, to overthrow</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(people)</i> to begin to throng; <i>(snow)</i> to begin to fall heavily, to begin to fall in thick flakes; <i>(smoke)</i> to begin to belch</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>ли́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поваля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend some time rolling about or wallowing

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend some time lying about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a person — idly or due to illness; of objects — due to being carelessly strewn</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поваля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
